Tonk card game is challenging and fun game for everyone\r\n\r\nIt is a quick game with relatively straightforward rules.\r\n\r\nIts objective is to eliminate your cards by forming them into ‘spreads’, meaning either 3 or 4 identical cards, or 3 or more sequentially in the same suit. During the game a player may add to their own spread, or an opponent’s spread. Play ends when a player has no cards left.\r\n\r\nTonk is a matching card game.
